ID: T33.G7.04
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Understand service authorization and keep shared URLs private
Description: Students learn that CreatiCode's Cloud and AI blocks handle authentication automatically through the platform. They understand that shared Google Sheet/Drive URLs grant access to anyone with the link and should not be publicly posted with sensitive data. They document best practices: use test data in shared sheets, avoid storing personal information, and understand that URL sharing is equivalent to granting access.

Dependencies:
* T08.G5.01: Use nested conditionals for multi-branch decisions
* T31.G5.01: Trace how a device reaches an online service
* T33.G6.05: Handle latency and error states in service calls
* T33.G6.06: Respect usage limits and rate limiting


ID: T33.G7.05
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Build workflows that combine multiple services
Description: Learners orchestrate multi-service workflows: fetch web content → process with AI → store results in Google Sheets, or read settings from Sheets → generate AI content → display. They handle intermediate data and ensure each step completes before the next begins.

Dependencies:
* T06.G5.01: Use broadcast for sprite-to-sprite communication
* T09.G5.01: Create and use a numeric variable for score or count
* T31.G5.01: Trace how a device reaches an online service
* T33.G6.06: Respect usage limits and rate limiting


ID: T33.G7.06
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Compare service options and pick the right tool
Description: Students analyze requirements and select the appropriate block: Google Sheets for structured persistent data, web fetch for external content, AI blocks for generation/analysis. They justify choices based on capabilities, latency, and data format.

Dependencies:
* T08.G5.01: Use nested conditionals for multi-branch decisions
* T31.G5.01: Trace how a device reaches an online service
* T33.G6.05: Handle latency and error states in service calls
* T33.G6.06: Respect usage limits and rate limiting


ID: T33.G7.07
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Use tables to cache service data and reduce repeated requests
Description: Learners store previous request/response pairs in a CreatiCode table and check the cache before making external Cloud or AI calls. This reduces service calls, improves performance, and respects rate limits. They implement simple cache expiration using timestamps for data that may change, clearing cached entries after a set duration.

Dependencies:
* T09.G5.01: Create and use a numeric variable for score or count
* T10.G5.01: Store related values in a list
* T31.G5.01: Trace how a device reaches an online service
* T33.G6.05: Handle latency and error states in service calls


ID: T33.G8.01
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Insert and remove rows and columns dynamically in Google Sheets
Description: Students use `insert rows`, `insert columns`, `remove rows`, and `remove columns` blocks to dynamically resize spreadsheet data areas. They build data management systems that archive old data by removing rows, expand storage by inserting new rows/columns, and reorganize datasets. This extends G7.01's sheet-level structure management to cell-range-level manipulation.

Dependencies:
* T08.G6.01: Use conditionals to control simulation steps
* T10.G6.01: Sort a table by a column
* T31.G6.01: Trace the steps of an HTTP/HTTPS request
* T33.G7.01: Manage Google Sheets structure programmatically
* T33.G7.02: Perform targeted Google Sheets cell operations

ID: T33.G8.05
Topic: T33 – Connected Services & Tool Wrappers
Skill: Decide when to use a service block versus building functionality yourself
Description: Learners evaluate tradeoffs when choosing between Cloud/AI blocks and custom solutions: internet dependency, response time, data persistence, and complexity. They analyze scenarios like Google Sheets vs local tables for data storage, web fetch vs pre-entered data for content, AI generation vs pre-made assets for media. They document their reasoning and justify their choices.

Dependencies:

Description: Students build a complete data pipeline as a capstone: fetch external data → process and transform → store in Google Sheets → use in AI calls → save AI outputs back to cloud. They handle errors at each stage, implement logging, and create a dashboard showing pipeline status.

Dependencies:
* T06.G6.01: Trace event execution paths in a multi‑event program
* T10.G6.01: Sort a table by a column
* T31.G6.01: Trace the steps of an HTTP/HTTPS request

Description: Students debate policy scenarios (device-free times, notifications) referencing evidence on focus and health.

ID: T35.G5.03
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Analyze AI's differential impacts on workers and communities
Description: Learners research how AI affects different communities unequally: which jobs are most at risk, how impacts vary by education/income level, geographic disparities in AI adoption, and how T21-T24 AI tools might worsen or improve equity. They propose reskilling and policy solutions with social justice focus.

Dependencies:
* T04.G2.01: Identify the repeating unit in a longer pattern
* T35.G4.01: Analyze case studies of tech helping/harming communities
* T35.G3.02: Discuss how algorithms influence what we see

ID: T35.G6.02
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Analyze data privacy tradeoffs
Description: Learners read mock privacy statements and decide whether the data collection is justified for the feature.

Dependencies:
* T35.G5.01: Examine global impacts of technology
* T35.G4.02: Understand advertising/persuasion online


ID: T35.G6.03
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Develop comprehensive AI ethics guidelines for T21-T24 applications
Description: Students create comprehensive ethical guidelines covering all T21-T24 AI applications: T21 image generation (bias, consent, cultural representation), T22 chatbots (privacy, misinformation, accessibility), T23 perception (consent, surveillance concerns, equity), and T24 XO assistance (academic integrity, citation, dependency). They connect guidelines to social justice principles and equity outcomes.

Dependencies:
* T35.G5.03: Analyze AI's differential impacts on workers and communities
* T35.G4.03: Reflect on accessibility/inclusion in games


ID: T35.G6.04
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics

* T35.G4.01: Analyze case studies of tech helping/harming communities


ID: T35.G7.01
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Conduct comprehensive bias audits across T21-T24 AI features
Description: Students systematically audit T21 image generation (representation across demographics), T22 chatbots (response quality by dialect/topic), T23 perception (accuracy by skin tone/lighting), and T24 XO assistance (help quality by English proficiency). They measure disparities, analyze root causes, and propose both technical and policy solutions.

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.03: Develop comprehensive AI ethics guidelines for T21-T24 applications
* T35.G5.03: Analyze AI's differential impacts on workers and communities


ID: T35.G7.02
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Explore unintended consequences of new tech
Description: Learners storyboard a technology (delivery drones, facial recognition) showing both intended use and unforeseen impact, then propose mitigations.

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.01: Apply ethics lenses (beneficence, fairness, autonomy)
* T35.G5.01: Examine global impacts of technology


ID: T35.G7.03
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Evaluate transparency vs security tensions
Description: Students weigh openness (auditability) against misuse risks for a hypothetical AI tool and justify a recommendation.

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.02: Analyze data privacy tradeoffs
* T35.G5.02: Debate digital well-being scenarios


ID: T35.G7.04
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Analyze societal impacts of AI perception technologies (Pairing with T23)
Description: Following T23 perception projects, students analyze real-world case studies of AI surveillance (facial recognition in schools, emotion detection at work, gesture tracking in public). They debate tradeoffs between security and privacy, examine disproportionate impacts on marginalized communities, and propose ethical guidelines.

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.02: Analyze data privacy tradeoffs
* T35.G6.03: Develop comprehensive AI ethics guidelines for T21-T24 applications


ID: T35.G7.05
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics
Skill: Debate ethical implications of AI media generation (Pairing with T21)
Description: Following T21 AI media projects, students hold structured debates on AI's impact on artists, photographers, and designers. They examine issues of copyright, style imitation, job displacement, cultural representation in training data, and propose frameworks for ethical AI media use.

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.03: Develop comprehensive AI ethics guidelines for T21-T24 applications
* T35.G5.03: Analyze AI's differential impacts on workers and communities


ID: T35.G7.06
Topic: T35 – Impacts & Ethics

Dependencies:
* T35.G6.04: Examine digital divide data

Dependencies:
* T35.G7.01: Conduct comprehensive bias audits across T21-T24 AI features
